Overview Notes: Please remember to get you dermatology review done - you have a family history of Melanoma and this puts you at a significant increased risk of developing one yourself

Overview Notes: Sinus bradycardia on ECG ; Possible vascular disease (abnormal ABI on the right)
Annual Dermatology review; Slightly raised cholesterol
Comment Key: MedicalHistoryRecommendation
Comment Value: -Continue annual health screening. Pay attention to the conditions that have occurred in your family. Employ lifestyle habits that improve & benefit your present & future health.
Special Investigation Notes: Urine - Protein trace
